[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run against the POIFSDump utility in Apache POI triggered a        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         critical security finding: a File Path Traversal issue. The fuzzer invoked          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         POIFSDump with a crafted input path containing “..[35m/[0m” sequences, which led to        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         detection by the `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer. This indicates that unvalidated     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path segments in POIFSDump can be exploited to traverse directories beyond the      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intended input location.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Observed                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           During fuzz testing of the `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer` harness, the input path passed to [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIFSDump.dump` included “..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”. The Jazzer sanitizer      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal` intercepted this        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sequence and raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`, flagging it as a file path     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal attempt.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The sanitizer explicitly identifies this as a “File path traversal”               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability. Such vulnerabilities allow an attacker to influence file-system      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         paths in a way that escapes the intended directory boundaries, potentially exposing [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         or overwriting arbitrary files.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Key Observations                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception originates in `FilePathTraversal.check` and propagates through    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `checkPath` and `pathFirstArgHook`, indicating the sanitizer is applied to the      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         first argument of the file-path–handling methods.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The target under test is `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump`, invoked by  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         its `main` method in `POIFSDump.java`, and driven by the fuzzer harness at          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The printed path in the exception message [1m([0m`Root                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m shows that relative path components are not    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalized or restricted before being used.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           To fully assess the scope of this issue, the following should be reviewed:        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. The argument handling in `POIFSDump.dump` and `POIFSDump.main`, to see how     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         file paths are read, concatenated, or resolved.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Any utility or helper methods in Apache POI that perform path normalization or [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         canonicalization on user-supplied input.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. The fuzzer harness [1m([0m`POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer`[1m)[0m to understand how inputs are         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         constructed and whether additional paths or file-handling code exist elsewhere in   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the POI codebase that might be similarly affected.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The interaction between POI’s file-reading logic [1m([0me.g., POIFS filesystem       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         access[1m)[0m and any platform-specific path resolution behavior.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         No root-cause diagnosis or remediation steps are included in this report.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalize and assign `baseDumpPath`:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     baseDumpPath = [0m[1;35mdumpDir.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create the root directory safely:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     File rootDir = [0m[1;35mresolveSafeFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mroot.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mrootDir.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mrootDir.mkdirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Could not create directory "[0m[39m + rootDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot, rootDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Remove any inline normalize/startsWith code already attempted—use the helper [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry, File[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for directories and document entries  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In the `public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry root, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. For DirectoryEntry recursion:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String name = [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      File subdir = [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mresolveSafeFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDumpPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35msubdir.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35msubdir.mkdirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Could not create directory "[0m[39m + subdir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir, subdir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Actually, since `resolveSafeFile` resolves against `baseDumpPath`, compute [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct relative path:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Compute the entry's path under the dump root[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      java.nio.file.Path parentRel = [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mbaseDumpPath.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      File subdir = [0m[1;35mresolveSafeFile[0m[1;39m([0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mparentRel.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. For DocumentNode entries:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String filename = [0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      java.nio.file.Path parentRel = [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mbaseDumpPath.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      File outFile = [0m[1;35mresolveSafeFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparentRel.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream out = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35moutFile.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mout.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOIFSFileSystem, int, String, File[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In the `public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOIFSFileSystem fs, int startBlock, String name,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFile parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Compute safe output file path[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   java.nio.file.Path parentRel = [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mbaseDumpPath.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   File outFile = [0m[1;35mresolveSafeFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparentRel.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure parent directories exist[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35moutFile.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream out = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35moutFile.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       POIFSStream stream = new [0m[1;35mPOIFSStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfs, startBlock[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m existing stream-writing logic [0m[33m...[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing IO logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrimming names, reading bytes, recursing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The helper enforces the same prefix-check for every file/directory creation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msite, subsuming the previously incomplete ad-hoc patches.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Factorizing path normalization and prefix checks reduces code duplication and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensures consistency across all write sites.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Using a single `baseDumpPath` anchored at `<input>_dump` guarantees that no “..” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor absolute names can escape the intended directory tree.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Throwing `IOException` on invalid entry names preserves the original behavior of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailing fast on directory creation errors.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The approach does not modify any harness or fuzzing logic, nor external [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries—only POIFSDump.java is touched.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Similar pattern is applied elsewhere in POI [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in `[0m[1;35mPOIXMLDocument.write[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor safe file serialization.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Relative path computation via `relativize` must not throw exceptions; ensure that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is always within `baseDumpPath` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguaranteed by the resolver on [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe way in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If users rely on processing some malformed names [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., with embedded “..”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthose entries now cause a full dump abort. Given this is a developer utility, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhalting is acceptable for security.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Thoroughly test with valid nested entries to confirm no regression in directory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlayout.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to harness or test code; existing tests for POIFSDump should continue [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto pass.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
